 Doordarshan was established on 15 September 1959
 2
 The first news bulletin was broadcast from Doordarshan on August 15, 1965 and the journey continues till today
 3
 Till 1975 it was limited to only 7 cities
 4

 6

 7

 Election campaigning before voting is at its peak
 shivasena ne yahaan se maujuuda saansad rajendra gavit ko ummidavaar banaaya he, jabaki raajnneetik sameekaran ke maddenjar congress-ensipi gathbandhan ne yah seat bahujan vikaas aghadi ke liye chhod di he
 Aghadi has given ticket to former MP Baliram Jadhav from here
 darasal palghar loksabhaa seat 2008 main hue parisemen ke baad astitv main ai thi
 In the recent Lok Sabha by-election here, BJP won a tough fight, Rajendra Gavit became MP
 unhone shivasena ke shrinivas chintaman vanaga ko chunaav haraaya
 The interesting thing in this election was that the BJP and Shiv Sena, which contested in the alliance in 2014, had gone face to face in the Palghar by-election
 iske pehle 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main yahaan se saansad chintaman vanaga chunaav jite the
 He defeated Baliram Jadhav of Bahujan Vikas Aghadi
 is chunaav main chintaman vanaga ne 5,33,201 vot hasil kiye
 While Baliram Jadhav got 2,93,681 votes
 vahiin, 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaav kii baat kii jaae to bahujan vikaas aghadi se baliram jadhav jite the
 He defeated Chintaman Wanaga
 kya rahaa he palghar loksabhaa seat kaa itihaas
 
 
 Prior to delimitation, Palghar Lok Sabha constituency was under Dahanu, while vasai-virar area was part of North Mumbai Lok Sabha
 dahanu loksabhaa kii baat kii jaae to yahaan 1967 main yashwantrao maartandrav mukane chunaav jitkar sansad pahunche
 After that, in 1977, Kom Shivadva won elections from Communist Party of India (M)
 phir congress ke damodar shingada lagaataar 1980, 1984, 1989 or 1991 main chunaav jite
 Then Chintaman Vanaga of BJP managed to win the victory here in 1996
 1998 main shankar sakhaaraam congress se jite
 Chintaman Vanaga won from BJP in 1999
 2004 main damodar barku shingada jeetne main kaamyaab rahe

 palghar adivasee bahul ilaaka he

 'humons of bombai' ne apane fasebuk pej par mumbai kii is ladki kii kahani share kii he, jo na keval is yuva dancer kii takalifon or sangharsh ko bayaan karti he, balki uski maa kii majboot ichhashakti, sangharsh or jijeevishaa ko bhi saamne laati he
 
 
 This story tells us how a mother tries to write the story of her golden future in an unknown world, leaving everything behind for the better future of her children
 darasal, is post main yah yuva dancer bataati he - "jab main saat saal kii thi, tab mujhe vah sab dekhnaa padaa, jise dekhnaa kisi bachche ke naseeb main nahin hona chahie
 
 
 My father was an alcoholic, beating my mother almost daily
 
 
 alag-alag dharmon ke hone ke baavjood mere mata-pita ne prem vivaah kiya tha, lekin vastav main us ghar main meri maa ko kabhi bhi sweekaar nahin kiya gaya

 My father's mother never adopted me or my sister
 
 
 vah hamen is tarah nazarandaaz karti thi, jaise hamaara koi astitv hi nahin he

 or kabhi-kabhi kisi or bekaar vajah se bhi, or yah silsilaa saat saal tak chalata rahaa
 
 
 " is yuva nartki ke mutabik - "meri maa ko kaam karne kii bhi ijazat nahin di jaati thi, isliye vah hamen (donon bacchiyon ko) kuch bhi dilaane ke liye 10-10 rupee kii 'bheekh' mere pita se maangati thi
 
 
 i still feel guilty for this, because i saw all this happening in front of my eyes, and did nothing
 
 
 main sirf apni choti bahan ko seene se laga leti thi or roti rahati thi
 
 
 " iske baad vah likhti he - "ek raat mere pita ne maa ko itani buree tarah peeta ki halaat bardaasht se baahar ho gaye
 
 
 Then the mother picked up our two sisters at 2 o'clock in the night, and at night we all came out on the street without shoes and money
 
 
 ham ek sthaneey baar main gaye, jo us vakt bhi khulaa hua tha
 
 
 My mother requested the bar owner to let me make a phone call, which she immediately accepted
 
 
 us baar maalik ne hamen khaanaa khilaane kii peshkash bhi di
 
 
 " ladki bataati he - "iske baad meri maa ke mata-pita aakar hamen apane saath le gaye, or uske baad se ab tak us parivaar (pita ke parivaar) ko hamane dobaaraa kabhi nahin dekha
 
 
 The father died a few years later, but even then nothing has changed for us regarding that family
 
 
 meri maa or naanaa-nani ne hamaara skool to badla hi, is ummid main hamaare naam bhi badal die ki shaayad isse ham pichhali zindagi bhul saken, or hamaari nai zindagi shuru ho
 
 
 " yaadon main duubati-utaraati yah ladki aage likhti he - "kabhi-kabhi main skool main teacher ko saamne khadaa dekhakar hi ronaa shuru kar detii thi

 aath saal kii umr se hi main nrity kar rahi hum
 
 
 "comments iske aage vah bataati he - "meri maa hamen paalane-posane ke liye din-raat kaam karti thi, or bhale hi itane lambey arase tak unhen bandishon main rakhaa gaya tha, unhone hamen kuch bhi padhane-seekhney kii puri azaadi di
 
 
 i have won the Belly Dancing Competition by going to China, and i have been performing all over the country, and my mother has never stopped me

 meraa pita sharaabi tha, jo lagbhag rose meri maa ko peethta tha

 mere pita kii maa ne mujhe yaa meri bahan ko kabhi god main nahin liya

 har raat meraa pita sharaab peetaa, or is vajah se meri maa ko peethta, kyonki usne betiyaan paidaa kii thim

 " According to this young dancer - "my mother was not even allowed to work, so she used to ask me (both girls) 'begging' of 10-10 rupees to get us anything
" 
 
 main aaj bhi is baat ke liye khud ko doshi mahasoos karti hum, kyonki maine yah sab apni ankhon ke saamne ghatate dekha, or kuch bhi nahin kiya
